v0.7.0 (September 11, 2018)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#v0-7-0-september-11-2018 "Permalink to this headline")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Warning

Google finance and Morningstar for historical price data have been immediately deprecated.

Highlights include:

*   Immediate deprecation of Google finance and Morningstar for historical price data, as these API endpoints are no longer supported by their respective providers. Alternate methods are welcome via pull requests, as PDR would like to restore these features.
    
*   Removal of EDGAR, which was deprecated in v0.6.0.
    

What’s new in v0.7.0

*   [Enhancements](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-070-enhancements)
    
*   [Backwards incompatible API changes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-070-api-breaking)
    
*   [Bug Fixes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-070-bug-fixes)
    

### Enhancements[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-070-enhancements "Permalink to this headline")

*   A new data connector for data provided by [Alpha Vantage](https://www.alphavantage.co/documentation)
     was introduced to obtain Foreign Exchange (FX) data. ([GH389](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/389)
    )
    
*   A new data connector for data provided by [Alpha Vantage](https://www.alphavantage.co/documentation)
     was introduced to obtain historical time series data. ([GH389](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/389)
    )
    
*   A new data connector for data provided by
    
    [Alpha Vantage](https://www.alphavantage.co/documentation)
     was introduced to obtain sector performance data, accessed through the top-level function `get_sector_performance_av`. ([GH389](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/389)
    )
    
*   A new data connector for data provided by [Alpha Vantage](https://www.alphavantage.co/documentation)
     was introduced to obtain real-time Batch Stock Quotes through the top-level function `get_quote_av`. ([GH389](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/389)
    )
    
*   MOEX data connector now supports multiple symbols in constructor. ([GH562](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/562)
    )
    

### Backwards incompatible API changes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-070-api-breaking "Permalink to this headline")

*   Deprecation of Google finance daily reader. Google retired the remaining financial data end point in June 2018. It is not possible to reliably retrieve historical price data without this endpoint. The Google daily reader will raise an ImmediateDeprecationError when called.
    
*   Deprecation of Morningstar daily reader. Morningstar ended support for the historical price data endpoint in July 2018. It is not possible to retrieve historical price data without this endpoint. The Morningstar daily reader will raise an ImmediateDeprecationError when called.
    
*   When requesting multiple symbols from a DailyReader (ex: google, yahoo, IEX) a MultiIndex DataFrame is now returned. Previously Panel or dict of DataFrames were returned. ([GH297](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/297)
    ).
    

### Bug Fixes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-070-bug-fixes "Permalink to this headline")

*   Fixed import of pandas.compat ([GH657](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/657)
    )
    
*   Added support for passing the API KEY to QuandlReader either directly or by setting the environmental variable QUANDL\_API\_KEY ([GH485](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/485)
    ).
    
*   Added support for optionally passing a custom base\_url to the EnigmaReader ([GH499](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/499)
    ).
    
*   Fix Yahoo! price data ([GH498](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/498)
    ).
    
*   Added back support for Yahoo! price, dividends, and splits data for stocks and currency pairs ([GH487](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/487)
    ).
    
*   Add is\_list\_like to compatibility layer to avoid failure on pandas >= 0.23 ([GH520](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/520)
    ).
    
*   Fixed Yahoo! time offset ([GH487](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/487)
    ).
    
*   Fix Yahoo! quote reader ([GH540](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/540)
    ).
    
*   Remove import of deprecated tm.get\_data\_path ([GH566](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/566)
    )
    
*   Allow full usage of stooq url parameters.
    
*   Removed unused requests-file and requests-ftp dependencies.
    
*   Fix Yahoo! actions issue where the default reporting adjusts dividends. The unadjusted dividends may lack precision due to accumulated numerical error when converting adjusted to the original dividend amount. ([GH495](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/495)
    )
    

v0.6.0 (January 24, 2018)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#v0-6-0-january-24-2018 "Permalink to this headline")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a major release from 0.5.0. We recommend that all users upgrade.

Warning

Yahoo!, Google Options, Google Quotes and EDGAR have been immediately deprecated.

Note

Google finance is still functioning for historical price data, although there are frequent reports of failures. Failure is frequently encountered when bulk downloading historical price data.

Highlights include:

*   Immediate deprecation of Yahoo!, Google Options and Quotes and EDGAR. The end points behind these APIs have radically changed and the existing readers require complete rewrites. In the case of most Yahoo! data the endpoints have been removed. PDR would like to restore these features, and pull requests are welcome.
    
*   A new connector for Tiingo was introduced. Tiingo provides historical end-of-day data for a large set of equities, ETFs and mutual funds. Free registration is required to get an API key ([GH478](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/478)
    ).
    
*   A new connector for Robinhood was introduced. This provides up to 1 year of historical end-of-day data. It also provides near real-time quotes. ([GH477](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/477)
    ).
    
*   A new connector for Morningstar Open, High, Low, Close and Volume was introduced ([GH467](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/467)
    )
    
*   A new connector for IEX daily price data was introduced ([GH465](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/465)
    ).
    
*   A new connector for IEX the majority of the IEX API was introduced ([GH446](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/446)
    ).
    
*   A new data connector for stock index data provided by Stooq was introduced ([GH447](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/447)
    ).
    
*   A new data connector for data provided by the Bank of Canada was introduced ([GH440](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/440)
    ).
    
*   A new data connector for data provided by Moscow Exchange (MOEX) introduced ([GH381](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/381)
    ).
    

What’s new in v0.6.0

*   [Enhancements](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-060-enhancements)
    
*   [Backwards incompatible API changes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-060-api-breaking)
    
*   [Bug Fixes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-060-bug-fixes)
    
*   [Other Changes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#other-changes)
    

### Enhancements[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-060-enhancements "Permalink to this headline")

*   A new data connector for data provided by the [Bank of Canada](https://www.bankofcanada.ca/rates/)
     was introduced. ([GH440](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/440)
    )
    
*   A new data connector for stock index data provided by [Stooq](https://stooq.com/)
     was introduced. ([GH447](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/447)
    )
    
*   A new connector for IEX the majority of the [IEX API](https://iextrading.com/developer/docs/)
     was introduced ([GH446](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/446)
    ).
    
*   A new connector for [IEX daily price data](https://iextrading.com/developer/docs/)
     was introduced ([GH465](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/465)
    ).
    
*   A new data connector for stock pricing data provided by [Morningstar](http://www.morningstar.com/)
     was introduced. ([GH467](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/467)
    )
    
*   A new data connector for stock pricing data provided by [Robinhood](https://www.robinhood.com/)
     was introduced. ([GH477](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/477)
    )
    
*   A new data connector for stock pricing data provided by [Tiingo](https://api.tiingo.com/docs)
     was introduced. ([GH478](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/478)
    )
    
*   A new data connector for data provided by [Moscow Exchange](https://iss.moex.com/iss/reference/?lang=en)
     was introduced. ([GH381](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/381)
    ).
    

### Backwards incompatible API changes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-060-api-breaking "Permalink to this headline")

*   Deprecation of Yahoo readers. Yahoo! retired the financial data end points in late 2017. It is not possible to reliably retrieve data from Yahoo! without these endpoints. The Yahoo! readers have been immediately deprecated and will raise an ImmediateDeprecationError when called.
    
*   Deprecation of EDGAR readers. EDGAR substantially altered their API. The EDGAR readers have been immediately deprecated and will raise an ImmediateDeprecationError when called.
    
*   Google finance data will raise an UnstableAPIWarning when first called. Google has also altered their API in a way that makes reading data unreliable. It many call it works. However it also regularly fails, especially when used for bulk downloading. Google may be removed in the future.
    

### Bug Fixes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-060-bug-fixes "Permalink to this headline")

*   freq parameter was added to the WorldBank connector to address a limitation ([GH198](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/198)
    , [GH449](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/449)
    ).
    
*   The Enigma data connector was updated to the latest API ([GH380](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/380)
    ).
    
*   The Google finance endpoint was updated to the latest value ([GH404](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/404)
    ).
    
*   Tne end point for FRED was updated to the latest values ([GH436](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/436)
    ).
    
*   Tne end point for WorldBank was updated to the latest values ([GH456](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/456)
    ).
    

### Other Changes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/whatsnew.html#other-changes "Permalink to this headline")

*   The minimum tested pandas version was increased to 0.19.2 ([GH441](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/441)
    ).
    
*   Added versioneer to simplifying release ([GH442](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/442)
    ).
    
*   Added doctr to automatically build docs for gh-pages ([GH459](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/459)
    ).

# Other Data Sources — pandas-datareader 0.10.0 documentation

#### Previous topic

[Caching queries](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/cache.html "previous chapter")

#### Next topic

[Data Readers](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/readers/index.html "next chapter")

### Quick search

   

On this page

Other Data Sources[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/see-also.html#other-data-sources "Permalink to this headline")

========================================================================================================================================

Web interfaces are constantly evolving and so there is constant evolution in this space. There are a number of noteworthy Python packages that integrate into the PyData ecosystem that are more narrowly focused than pandas-datareader.

Alpha Vantage[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/see-also.html#alpha-vantage "Permalink to this headline")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Alpha Vantage](https://www.alphavantage.co/)
 provides real time and historical equity data. Users are required to get a free API key before using the API. [Documentation](https://www.alphavantage.co/documentation)
 is available.

A [python package](https://github.com/RomelTorres/alpha_vantage)
 simplifying access is available on github.

Tiingo[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/see-also.html#tiingo "Permalink to this headline")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Tiingo](https://www.tiingo.com/)
 aims to make high-end financial tools accessible investors. The [API is documented](https://api.tiingo.com/)
. Users are required to get a free API key before using the API.

A [python package](https://github.com/hydrosquall/tiingo-python)
 simplifying access is available on github.

Barchart[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/see-also.html#barchart "Permalink to this headline")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Barchart is a data provider covering a wide range of financial data. The [free API](https://www.barchart.com/ondemand/free-market-data-api)
 provides up to two years of historical data.

A [python package](https://github.com/femtotrader/barchart-ondemand-client-python)
 simplifying access is available on github.

List of Other Sources[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/see-also.html#list-of-other-sources "Permalink to this headline")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Awesome Quant](https://github.com/wilsonfreitas/awesome-quant#data-sources)
 maintains a large list of packages designed to provide access to financial data.

[Caching queries](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/cache.html "previous page")
 [Data Readers](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/readers/index.html "next page")

---

# AlphaVantage — pandas-datareader 0.10.0 documentation

#### Previous topic

[Data Readers](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/index.html "previous chapter")

#### Next topic

[Federal Reserve Economic Data (FRED)](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/fred.html "next chapter")

### Quick search

   

AlphaVantage[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#module-pandas_datareader.av.forex "Permalink to this headline")

=============================================================================================================================================================

_class_ `pandas_datareader.av.forex.``AVForexReader`(_symbols=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_, _api\_key=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader "Permalink to this definition")

Returns DataFrame of the Alpha Vantage Foreign Exchange (FX) Exchange Rates data.

New in version 0.7.0.

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_string__,_ _array-like object_ _(_[_list_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ [_tuple_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _Series__)_) – Single currency pair (formatted ‘FROM/TO’) or list of the same.
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used
    
*   **api\_key** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_) – Alpha Vantage API key . If not provided the environmental variable ALPHAVANTAGE\_API\_KEY is read. The API key is _required_.
    

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

`data_key`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader.data_key "Permalink to this definition")

Key of data returned from Alpha Vantage

`default_start_date`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader.default_start_date "Permalink to this definition")

Default start date for reader. Defaults to 5 years before current date

`function`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader.function "Permalink to this definition")

Alpha Vantage endpoint function

`params`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader.params "Permalink to this definition")

Parameters to use in API calls

`read`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader.read "Permalink to this definition")

Read data from connector

`url`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.forex.AVForexReader.url "Permalink to this definition")

API URL

_class_ `pandas_datareader.av.time_series.``AVTimeSeriesReader`(_symbols=None_, _function='TIME\_SERIES\_DAILY'_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_, _chunksize=25_, _api\_key=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/alphavantage.html#pandas_datareader.av.time_series.AVTimeSeriesReader "Permalink to this definition")

Returns DataFrame of the Alpha Vantage Stock Time Series endpoints

New in version 0.7.0.

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_string_) – Single stock symbol (ticker)
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Defaults to 20 years before current date.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used
    
*   **api\_key** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_) – AlphaVantage API key . If not provided the environmental variable ALPHAVANTAGE\_API\_KEY is read. The API key is _required_.

_class_ `pandas_datareader.yahoo.daily.``YahooDailyReader`(_symbols=None_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_, _adjust\_price=False_, _ret\_index=False_, _chunksize=1_, _interval='d'_, _get\_actions=False_, _adjust\_dividends=True_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.daily.YahooDailyReader "Permalink to this definition")

Returns DataFrame of with historical over date range, start to end. To avoid being penalized by Yahoo! Finance servers, pauses between downloading ‘chunks’ of symbols can be specified.

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_string__,_ _array-like object_ _(_[_list_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ [_tuple_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _Series__)__, or_ _DataFrame_) – Single stock symbol (ticker), array-like object of symbols or DataFrame with index containing stock symbols.
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Defaults to 5 years before current date.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used. Passing a session is an advanced usage and you must set any required headers in the session directly.
    
*   **adjust\_price** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default False_) – If True, adjusts all prices in hist\_data (‘Open’, ‘High’, ‘Low’, ‘Close’) based on ‘Adj Close’ price. Adds ‘Adj\_Ratio’ column and drops ‘Adj Close’.
    
*   **ret\_index** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default False_) – If True, includes a simple return index ‘Ret\_Index’ in hist\_data.
    
*   **chunksize** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 25_) – Number of symbols to download consecutively before intiating pause.
    
*   **interval** (_string__,_ _default 'd'_) – Time interval code, valid values are ‘d’ for daily, ‘w’ for weekly, ‘m’ for monthly.
    
*   **get\_actions** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default False_) – If True, adds Dividend and Split columns to dataframe.
    
*   **adjust\_dividends** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default true_) – If True, adjusts dividends for splits.
    

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.daily.YahooDailyReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

`default_start_date`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.daily.YahooDailyReader.default_start_date "Permalink to this definition")

_class_ `pandas_datareader.yahoo.fx.``YahooFXReader`(_symbols=None_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_, _adjust\_price=False_, _ret\_index=False_, _chunksize=1_, _interval='d'_, _get\_actions=False_, _adjust\_dividends=True_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.fx.YahooFXReader "Permalink to this definition")

Returns DataFrame of historical prices for currencies

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_string__,_ _array-like object_ _(_[_list_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ [_tuple_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _Series__)__, or_ _DataFrame_) – Single stock symbol (ticker), array-like object of symbols or DataFrame with index containing stock symbols.
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date, timestamp. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Defaults to ‘1/1/2010’.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date, timestamp. Same format as starting date. Defaults to today.
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used
    
*   **chunksize** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 25_ _(__NOT IMPLEMENTED__)_) – Number of symbols to download consecutively before intiating pause.
    
*   **interval** (_string__,_ _default '1d'_) –
    
    Valid values are ‘1d’, ‘5d’, ‘1mo’, ‘3mo’, ‘6mo’, ‘1y’, ‘2y’, ‘5y’,
    
    ’10y’, ‘ytd’, ‘max’
    

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.fx.YahooFXReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

`default_start_date`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.fx.YahooFXReader.default_start_date "Permalink to this definition")

Default start date for reader. Defaults to 5 years before current date

`params`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.fx.YahooFXReader.params "Permalink to this definition")

Parameters to use in API calls

`read`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.fx.YahooFXReader.read "Permalink to this definition")

Read data

`url`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.fx.YahooFXReader.url "Permalink to this definition")

API URL

_class_ `pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.``Options`(_symbol_, _session=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options "Permalink to this definition")

**\*Experimental\*** This class fetches call/put data for a given stock/expiry month.

It is instantiated with a string representing the ticker symbol.

The class has the following methods:

get\_options\_data(month, year, expiry) get\_call\_data(month, year, expiry) get\_put\_data(month, year, expiry) get\_near\_stock\_price(opt\_frame, above\_below) get\_all\_data(call, put) get\_forward\_data(months, call, put) (deprecated)

Examples

\# Instantiate object with ticker >>> aapl = Options(‘aapl’)

\# Fetch next expiry call data >>> calls = aapl.get\_call\_data()

\# Can now access aapl.calls instance variable >>> aapl.calls

\# Fetch next expiry put data >>> puts = aapl.get\_put\_data()

\# Can now access aapl.puts instance variable >>> aapl.puts

\# cut down the call data to be 3 below and 3 above the stock price. >>> cut\_calls = aapl.get\_near\_stock\_price(call=True, above\_below=3)

\# Fetch call and put data with expiry from now to 8 months out >>> forward\_data = aapl.get\_forward\_data(8, call=True, put=True)

\# Fetch all call and put data >>> all\_data = aapl.get\_all\_data()

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

`default_start_date`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.default_start_date "Permalink to this definition")

Default start date for reader. Defaults to 5 years before current date

`expiry_dates`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.expiry_dates "Permalink to this definition")

Returns a list of available expiry dates

`get_all_data`(_call=True_, _put=True_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.get_all_data "Permalink to this definition")

**\*Experimental\*** Gets either call, put, or both data for all available months starting in the current month.

Parameters

*   **call** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_ _(__default=True__)_) – Whether or not to collect data for call options
    
*   **put** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_ _(__default=True__)_) – Whether or not to collect data for put options.
    

Returns

*   _pandas.DataFrame_ – A DataFrame with requested options data.
    
    Index:
    
    Strike: Option strike, int Expiry: Option expiry, Timestamp Type: Call or Put, string Symbol: Option symbol as reported on Yahoo, string
    
    Columns:
    
    Last: Last option price, float Chg: Change from prior day, float PctChg: Change from prior day in percent, float Bid: Bid price, float Ask: Ask price, float Vol: Volume traded, int64 Open\_Int: Open interest, int64 IsNonstandard: True if the the deliverable is not 100 shares,
    
    > otherwise false
    
    Underlying: Ticker of the underlying security, string Underlying\_Price: Price of the underlying security, float64 Quote\_Time: Time of the quote, Timestamp Last\_Trade\_Date: Time of the last trade for this expiry
    
    > and strike, Timestamp
    
    IV: Implied volatility, float JSON: Parsed json object, json
    
    > Useful to extract other returned key/value pairs as needed
    
*   **Note** (_Format of returned DataFrame is dependent_) – on Yahoo and may change.
    

`get_call_data`(_month=None_, _year=None_, _expiry=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.get_call_data "Permalink to this definition")

**\*Experimental\*** Gets call/put data for the stock with the expiration data in the given month and year

Parameters

*   **month** (_number__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional__(__default=None__)_) – The month the options expire. This should be either 1 or 2 digits.
    
*   **year** (_number__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional__(__default=None__)_) – The year the options expire. This should be a 4 digit int.
    
*   **expiry** (_date-like_ _or_ _convertible or_) – list-like object, optional (default=None) The date (or dates) when options expire (defaults to current month)
    

Returns

**call\_data** – A DataFrame with requested options data.

Index:

Strike: Option strike, int Expiry: Option expiry, Timestamp Type: Call or Put, string Symbol: Option symbol as reported on Yahoo, string

Columns:

Last: Last option price, float Chg: Change from prior day, float PctChg: Change from prior day in percent, float Bid: Bid price, float Ask: Ask price, float Vol: Volume traded, int64 Open\_Int: Open interest, int64 IsNonstandard: True if the the deliverable is not 100 shares,

> otherwise false

Underlying: Ticker of the underlying security, string Underlying\_Price: Price of the underlying security, float64 Quote\_Time: Time of the quote, Timestamp Last\_Trade\_Date: Time of the last trade for this expiry

> and strike, Timestamp

IV: Implied volatility, float JSON: Parsed json object, json

> Useful to extract other returned key/value pairs as needed

Return type

pandas.DataFrame

Notes

Note: Format of returned DataFrame is dependent

on Yahoo and may change.

When called, this function will add instance variables named calls and puts. See the following example:

\>>> aapl \= Options('aapl', 'yahoo')  \# Create object
\>>> aapl.calls  \# will give an AttributeError
\>>> aapl.get\_call\_data()  \# Get data and set ivars
\>>> aapl.calls  \# Doesn't throw AttributeError

Also note that aapl.calls will always be the calls for the next expiry. If the user calls this method with a different month or year, the ivar will be named callsYYMMDD where YY, MM and DD are, respectively, two digit representations of the year, month and day for the expiry of the options.

`get_forward_data`(_months_, _call=True_, _put=False_, _near=False_, _above\_below=2_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.get_forward_data "Permalink to this definition")

**\*Experimental\*** Gets either call, put, or both data for months starting in the current month and going out in the future a specified amount of time.

Parameters

*   **months** (_number__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – How many months to go out in the collection of the data. This is inclusive.
    
*   **call** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_ _(__default=True__)_) – Whether or not to collect data for call options
    
*   **put** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_ _(__default=False__)_) – Whether or not to collect data for put options.
    
*   **near** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_ _(__default=False__)_) – Whether this function should get only the data near the current stock price. Uses Options.get\_near\_stock\_price
    
*   **above\_below** (_number__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_ _(__default=2__)_) – The number of strike prices above and below the stock price that should be taken if the near option is set to True
    

Returns

A DataFrame with requested options data.

Index:

Strike: Option strike, int Expiry: Option expiry, Timestamp Type: Call or Put, string Symbol: Option symbol as reported on Yahoo, string

Columns:

Last: Last option price, float Chg: Change from prior day, float PctChg: Change from prior day in percent, float Bid: Bid price, float Ask: Ask price, float Vol: Volume traded, int64 Open\_Int: Open interest, int64 IsNonstandard: True if the the deliverable is not 100 shares,

> otherwise false

Underlying: Ticker of the underlying security, string Underlying\_Price: Price of the underlying security, float64 Quote\_Time: Time of the quote, Timestamp Last\_Trade\_Date: Time of the last trade for this expiry

> and strike, Timestamp

IV: Implied volatility, float JSON: Parsed json object, json

> Useful to extract other returned key/value pairs as needed

Note: Format of returned DataFrame is dependent

on Yahoo and may change.

Return type

pandas.DataFrame

`get_near_stock_price`(_above\_below=2_, _call=True_, _put=False_, _month=None_, _year=None_, _expiry=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.get_near_stock_price "Permalink to this definition")

**\*Experimental\*** Returns a DataFrame of options that are near the current stock price.

    ) – Tells the function whether or not it should be using calls

Returns

**chopped** – The resultant DataFrame chopped down to be 2 \* above\_below + 1 rows

desired. If there isn’t data as far out as the user has asked for then

> otherwise false

`get_options_data`(_month=None_, _year=None_, _expiry=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/yahoo.html#pandas_datareader.yahoo.options.Options.get_options_data "Permalink to this definition")

**\*Experimental\*** Gets call/put data for the stock with the expiration data in the given month and year

Parameters

*   **month** (_number__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional__(__default=None__)_) – The month the options expire. This should be either 1 or 2 digits.
    
*   **year** (_number__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional__(__default=None__)_) – The year the options expire. This should be a 4 digit int.
    
*   **expiry** (_date-like_ _or_ _convertible or_) – list-like object, optional (default=None) The date (or dates) when options expire (defaults to current month)

A DataFrame with requested options data.

Index:

Strike: Option strike, int Expiry: Option expiry, Timestamp Type: Call or Put, string Symbol: Option symbol as reported on Yahoo, string

Columns:

Last: Last option price, float Chg: Change from prior day, float PctChg: Change from prior day in percent, float Bid: Bid price, float Ask: Ask price, float Vol: Volume traded, int64 Open\_Int: Open interest, int64 IsNonstandard: True if the the deliverable is not 100 shares,

> otherwise False

Underlying: Ticker of the underlying security, string Underlying\_Price: Price of the underlying security, float64 Quote\_Time: Time of the quote, Timestamp Last\_Trade\_Date: Time of the last trade for this expiry

> and strike, Timestamp

pandas.DataFrame

Notes

on Yahoo and may change.

When called, this function will add instance variables named calls and puts. See the following example:

\>>> aapl \= Options('aapl', 'yahoo')  \# Create object
\>>> aapl.calls  \# will give an AttributeError
\>>> aapl.get\_options()  \# Get data and set ivars
\>>> aapl.calls  \# Doesn't throw AttributeError

Also note that aapl.calls and appl.puts will always be the calls and puts for the next expiry. If the user calls this method with a different expiry, the ivar will be named callsYYMMDD or putsYYMMDD, where YY, MM and DD are, respectively, two digit representations of the year, month and day for the expiry of the options.

# The Investors Exchange (IEX) — pandas-datareader 0.10.0 documentation

#### Previous topic

[Eurostat](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/eurostat.html "previous chapter")

#### Next topic

[Moscow Exchange (MOEX)](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/moex.html "next chapter")

### Quick search

   

The Investors Exchange (IEX)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html#module-pandas_datareader.iex.daily "Permalink to this headline")

=====================================================================================================================================================================

_class_ `pandas_datareader.iex.daily.``IEXDailyReader`(_symbols=None_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_, _chunksize=25_, _api\_key=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html#pandas_datareader.iex.daily.IEXDailyReader "Permalink to this definition")

Returns DataFrame of historical stock prices from symbols, over date range, start to end. To avoid being penalized by IEX servers, pauses between downloading ‘chunks’ of symbols can be specified.

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_string__,_ _array-like object_ _(_[_list_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ [_tuple_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _Series__)__, or_ _DataFrame_) – Single stock symbol (ticker), array-like object of symbols or DataFrame with index containing stock symbols.
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Defaults to 15 years before current date
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **chunksize** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 25_) – Number of symbols to download consecutively before intiating pause.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used
    
*   **api\_key** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – IEX Cloud Secret Token
    

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html#pandas_datareader.iex.daily.IEXDailyReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

_class_ `pandas_datareader.iex.stats.``RecentReader`(_symbols=None_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html#pandas_datareader.iex.stats.RecentReader "Permalink to this definition")

Recent trading volume from IEX

Notes

Returns 6 fields for each day:

> *   date: refers to the trading day.
>     
> *   volume: refers to executions received from order routed to away trading centers.
>     
> *   routedVolume: refers to single counted shares matched from executions on IEX.
>     
> *   marketShare: refers to IEX’s percentage of total US Equity market volume.
>     
> *   isHalfday: will be true if the trading day is a half day.
>     
> *   litVolume: refers to the number of lit shares traded on IEX (single-counted).
>     

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html#pandas_datareader.iex.stats.RecentReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

_class_ `pandas_datareader.iex.deep.``Deep`(_symbols=None_, _service=None_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html#pandas_datareader.iex.deep.Deep "Permalink to this definition")

Retrieve order book data from IEX

Notes

Real-time depth of book quotations direct from IEX. Returns aggregated size of resting displayed orders at a price and side. Does not indicate the size or number of individual orders at any price level. Non-displayed orders and non-displayed portions of reserve orders are not counted.

Also provides last trade price and size information. Routed executions are not reported.

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html#pandas_datareader.iex.deep.Deep.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

# Enigma — pandas-datareader 0.10.0 documentation

#### Previous topic

[Econdb](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/econdb.html "previous chapter")

#### Next topic

[Eurostat](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/eurostat.html "next chapter")

### Quick search

   

Enigma[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/enigma.html#module-pandas_datareader.enigma "Permalink to this headline")

===============================================================================================================================================

_class_ `pandas_datareader.enigma.``EnigmaReader`(_dataset\_id=None_, _api\_key=None_, _retry\_count=5_, _pause=0.75_, _session=None_, _base\_url='https://public.enigma.com/api'_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/enigma.html#pandas_datareader.enigma.EnigmaReader "Permalink to this definition")

Collects current snapshot of Enigma data located at the specified data set ID and returns a pandas DataFrame.

Parameters

*   **dataset\_id** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – Enigma dataset UUID.
    
*   **api\_key** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_) – Enigma API key. If not provided, the environmental variable ENIGMA\_API\_KEY is read.
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 5_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_float_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, of the pause between retries.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used.
    
*   **base\_url** (str, optional (defaults to [https://public.enigma.com/api](https://public.enigma.com/api)
    )) – Alternative Enigma endpoint to be used.
    

Examples

Download current snapshot for the following Florida Inspections Dataset: [https://public.enigma.com/datasets/bedaf052-5fcd-4758-8d27-048ce8746c6a](https://public.enigma.com/datasets/bedaf052-5fcd-4758-8d27-048ce8746c6a)

\>>> import pandas\_datareader as pdr
\>>> df \= pdr.get\_data\_enigma('bedaf052-5fcd-4758-8d27-048ce8746c6a')

In the event that ENIGMA\_API\_KEY does not exist in your env, the key can be supplied as the second argument or as the keyword argument api\_key

\>>> df \= EnigmaReader(dataset\_id\='bedaf052-5fcd-4758-8d27-048ce8746c6a',
...                   api\_key\='INSERT\_API\_KEY').read()

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/enigma.html#pandas_datareader.enigma.EnigmaReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

`default_start_date`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/enigma.html#pandas_datareader.enigma.EnigmaReader.default_start_date "Permalink to this definition")

# Moscow Exchange (MOEX) — pandas-datareader 0.10.0 documentation

#### Previous topic

[The Investors Exchange (IEX)](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/iex.html "previous chapter")

#### Next topic

[NASDAQ](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/nasdaq-trader.html "next chapter")

### Quick search

   

Moscow Exchange (MOEX)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/moex.html#module-pandas_datareader.moex "Permalink to this headline")

===========================================================================================================================================================

_class_ `pandas_datareader.moex.``MoexReader`(_\*args_, _\*\*kwargs_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/moex.html#pandas_datareader.moex.MoexReader "Permalink to this definition")

Returns a DataFrame of historical stock prices from symbols from Moex

Parameters

*   **symbols** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _an array-like object_ _(_[_list_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ [_tuple_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _Series__)__, or_ _a DataFrame_) – A single stock symbol (secid), an array-like object of symbols or a DataFrame with an index containing stock symbols.
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Defaults to 20 years before current date.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – The number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **chunksize** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 25_) – The number of symbols to download consecutively before intiating pause.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used
    

Notes

To avoid being penalized by Moex servers, pauses more than 0.1s between downloading ‘chunks’ of symbols can be specified.

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/moex.html#pandas_datareader.moex.MoexReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

Default start date for reader. Defaults to 5 years before current date

# Quandl — pandas-datareader 0.10.0 documentation

#### Previous topic

[Organisation for Economic Co-operation and Development (OECD)](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/oecd.html "previous chapter")

#### Next topic

[Stooq.com](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/stooq.html "next chapter")

### Quick search

   

Quandl[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/quandl.html#module-pandas_datareader.quandl "Permalink to this headline")

===============================================================================================================================================

_class_ `pandas_datareader.quandl.``QuandlReader`(_symbols_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_, _chunksize=25_, _api\_key=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/quandl.html#pandas_datareader.quandl.QuandlReader "Permalink to this definition")

Returns DataFrame of historical stock prices from symbol, over date range, start to end.

New in version 0.5.0.

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_string_) – Possible formats: 1. DB/SYM: The Quandl ‘codes’: DB is the database name, SYM is a ticker-symbol-like Quandl abbreviation for a particular security. 2. SYM.CC: SYM is the same symbol and CC is an ISO country code, will try to map to the best single Quandl database for that country. Beware of ambiguous symbols (different securities per country)! Note: Cannot use more than a single string because of the inflexible way the URL is composed of url and \_get\_params in the superclass
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Defaults to 20 years before current date.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **chunksize** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 25_) – Number of symbols to download consecutively before intiating pause.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used
    
*   **api\_key** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_) – Quandl API key . If not provided the environmental variable QUANDL\_API\_KEY is read. The API key is _required_.
    

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/quandl.html#pandas_datareader.quandl.QuandlReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

`default_start_date`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/quandl.html#pandas_datareader.quandl.QuandlReader.default_start_date "Permalink to this definition")

Default start date for reader. Defaults to 5 years before current date

`params`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/quandl.html#pandas_datareader.quandl.QuandlReader.params "Permalink to this definition")

Parameters to use in API calls

`read`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/quandl.html#pandas_datareader.quandl.QuandlReader.read "Permalink to this definition")

Read data

### Quick search

   

World Bank[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#module-pandas_datareader.wb "Permalink to this headline")

===================================================================================================================================================

_class_ `pandas_datareader.wb.``WorldBankReader`(_symbols=None_, _countries=None_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _freq=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _session=None_, _errors='warn'_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.WorldBankReader "Permalink to this definition")

Download data series from the World Bank’s World Development Indicators

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_WorldBank indicator string_ _or_ _list of strings_) – taken from the `id` field in `WDIsearch()`
    
*   **countries** (_string_ _or_ _list of strings._) – `all` downloads data for all countries 2 or 3 character ISO country codes select individual countries (e.g.\`\`US\`\`,\`\`CA\`\`) or (e.g.\`\`USA\`\`,\`\`CAN\`\`). The codes can be mixed. The two ISO lists of countries, provided by wikipedia, are hardcoded into pandas as of 11/10/2014.
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – First year of the data series. Month and day are ignored.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Last year of the data series (inclusive). Month and day are ignored.
    
*   **errors** (_str {'ignore'__,_ _'warn'__,_ _'raise'}__,_ _default 'warn'_) – Country codes are validated against a hardcoded list. This controls the outcome of that validation, and attempts to also apply to the results from world bank. errors=’raise’, will raise a ValueError on a bad country code.
    

`close`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.WorldBankReader.close "Permalink to this definition")

Close network session

`default_start_date`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.WorldBankReader.default_start_date "Permalink to this definition")

Default start date for reader. Defaults to 5 years before current date

`get_countries`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.WorldBankReader.get_countries "Permalink to this definition")

Query information about countries

Notes

Provides information such as:

> *   country code
>     
> *   region
>     
> *   income level
>     
> *   capital city
>     
> *   latitude
>     
> *   and longitude
>     

`get_indicators`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.WorldBankReader.get_indicators "Permalink to this definition")

Read data

`search`(_string='gdp.\*capi'_, _field='name'_, _case=False_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.WorldBankReader.search "Permalink to this definition")

Search available data series from the world bank

Parameters

*   **string** (_string_) – regular expression
    
*   **field** (_string_) – id, name, source, sourceNote, sourceOrganization, topics See notes below
    
*   **case** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – case sensitive search?
    

Notes

The first time this function is run it will download and cache the full list of available series. Depending on the speed of your network connection, this can take time. Subsequent searches will use the cached copy, so they should be much faster.

id : Data series indicator (for use with the `indicator` argument of `WDI()`) e.g. NY.GNS.ICTR.GN.ZS” name: Short description of the data series source: Data collection project sourceOrganization: Data collection organization note: sourceNote: topics:

`url`[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.WorldBankReader.url "Permalink to this definition")

API URL

`pandas_datareader.wb.``download`(_country=None_, _indicator=None_, _start=2003_, _end=2005_, _freq=None_, _errors='warn'_, _\*\*kwargs_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.download "Permalink to this definition")

Download data series from the World Bank’s World Development Indicators

Parameters

*   **indicator** (_string_ _or_ _list of strings_) – taken from the `id` field in `WDIsearch()`
    
*   **country** (_string_ _or_ _list of strings._) –
    
    `all` downloads data for all countries 2 or 3 character ISO country codes select individual countries (e.g.\`\`US\`\`,\`\`CA\`\`) or (e.g.\`\`USA\`\`,\`\`CAN\`\`). The codes can be mixed.
    
    The two ISO lists of countries, provided by wikipedia, are hardcoded into pandas as of 11/10/2014.
    
*   **start** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – First year of the data series
    
*   **end** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – Last year of the data series (inclusive)
    
*   **freq** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – frequency or periodicity of the data to be retrieved (e.g. ‘M’ for monthly, ‘Q’ for quarterly, and ‘A’ for annual). None defaults to annual.
    
*   **errors** (_str {'ignore'__,_ _'warn'__,_ _'raise'}__,_ _default 'warn'_) – Country codes are validated against a hardcoded list. This controls the outcome of that validation, and attempts to also apply to the results from world bank. errors=’raise’, will raise a ValueError on a bad country code.
    
*   **kwargs** – keywords passed to WorldBankReader
    

Returns

**data** – DataFrame with columns country, year, indicator value

Return type

DataFrame

`pandas_datareader.wb.``get_countries`(_\*\*kwargs_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/world-bank.html#pandas_datareader.wb.get_countries "Permalink to this definition")

*   **case** ([_bool_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#bool "(in Python v3.9)")
    ) – case sensitive search?
    
*   **kwargs** – keywords passed to WorldBankReader
    

Notes

The first time this function is run it will download and cache the full list of available series. Depending on the speed of your network connection, this can take time. Subsequent searches will use the cached copy, so they should be much faster.

id : Data series indicator (for use with the `indicator` argument of `WDI()`) e.g. NY.GNS.ICTR.GN.ZS”

> *   name: Short description of the data series
>     
> *   source: Data collection project
>     
> *   sourceOrganization: Data collection organization
>     
> *   note:
>     
> *   sourceNote:
>     
> *   topics:
>

Returns DataFrame of historical TSP fund prices from symbols, over date range, start to end.

Parameters

*   **symbols** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _array-like object_ _(_[_list_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ [_tuple_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _Series__)__, or_ _DataFrame_) – Single stock symbol (ticker), array-like object of symbols or DataFrame with index containing stock symbols.
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Defaults to 20 years before current date.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, to pause between consecutive queries of chunks. If single value given for symbol, represents the pause between retries.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used

_class_ `pandas_datareader.tiingo.``TiingoDailyReader`(_symbols_, _start=None_, _end=None_, _retry\_count=3_, _pause=0.1_, _timeout=30_, _session=None_, _freq=None_, _api\_key=None_)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/tiingo.html#pandas_datareader.tiingo.TiingoDailyReader "Permalink to this definition")

Historical daily data from Tiingo on equities, ETFs and mutual funds

Parameters

*   **symbols** (_{str__,_ _List__\[_[_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")\
    _\]__}_) – String symbol or list of symbols
    
*   **start** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Starting date, timestamp. Parses many different kind of date representations (e.g., ‘JAN-01-2010’, ‘1/1/10’, ‘Jan, 1, 1980’). Default starting date is 5 years before current date.
    
*   **end** (_string__,_ [_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _date__,_ _datetime__,_ _Timestamp_) – Ending date, timestamp. Same format as starting date.
    
*   **retry\_count** ([_int_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 3_) – Number of times to retry query request.
    
*   **pause** ([_float_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#float "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _default 0.1_) – Time, in seconds, of the pause between retries.
    
*   **session** (_Session__,_ _default None_) – requests.sessions.Session instance to be used
    
*   **freq** (_{str__,_ _None}_) – Not used.
    
*   **api\_key** ([_str_](https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str "(in Python v3.9)")
    _,_ _optional_) – Tiingo API key . If not provided the environmental variable TIINGO\_API\_KEY is read. The API key is _required_.

    _\]__}_) – String symbol or list of symbols

`pandas_datareader.tiingo.``get_tiingo_symbols`()[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/latest/readers/tiingo.html#pandas_datareader.tiingo.get_tiingo_symbols "Permalink to this definition")

Get the set of stock symbols supported by Tiingo

Returns

**symbols** – DataFrame with symbols (ticker), exchange, asset type, currency and start and end dates

Return type

DataFrame

Notes

Reads [https://apimedia.tiingo.com/docs/tiingo/daily/supported\_tickers.zip](https://apimedia.tiingo.com/docs/tiingo/daily/supported_tickers.zip)

# What’s New — pandas-datareader 0.10.0 documentation

#### Previous topic

[Yahoo Finance](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/readers/yahoo.html "previous chapter")

### Quick search

   

On this page

What’s New[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#what-s-new "Permalink to this headline")

========================================================================================================================

These are new features and improvements of note in each release.

v0.10.0 (July 11, 2021)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#v0-10-0-july-11-2021 "Permalink to this headline")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Highlights include:

### Bug Fixes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#bug-fixes "Permalink to this headline")

*   Fixed Yahoo readers which now require headers
    
*   Fixed other reader
    
*   Improved compatibility with pandas
    

### Contributors[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#contributors "Permalink to this headline")

Thanks to all of the contributors for the 0.10.0 release (based on git log):

*   Kim Philipp Jablonski

*   Jeff Hale
    
*   Lukas Halim

*   Dmitry Alekseev
    

These lists of names are automatically generated based on git log, and may not be complete.

v0.9.1 (July 26, 2020)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#v0-9-1-july-26-2020 "Permalink to this headline")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Highlights include:

What’s new in v0.9.1

*   [Enhancements](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#enhancements)
    
*   [Bug Fixes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-091-bug-fixes)
    
*   [Contributors](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#id2)
    

### Enhancements[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#enhancements "Permalink to this headline")

*   MOEX now returns data only from primary trading boards for each ticker ([GH811](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/811)
    , [GH748](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/748)
    )
    
*   Added read\_all\_boards() method for MOEX that returns data from every trading board (ver. 0.9.0 behaviour)
    
*   Docs for MOEX reedited
    

### Bug Fixes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-091-bug-fixes "Permalink to this headline")

*   Fixed broken links on the github ussies on “What’s New” docs pages
    

### Contributors[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#id2 "Permalink to this headline")

*   Dmitry Alekseev
    

v0.9.0 (July 10, 2020)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#v0-9-0-july-10-2020 "Permalink to this headline")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Highlights include:

What’s new in v0.9.0

*   [Enhancements](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-090-enhancements)
    
*   [Backwards incompatible API changes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#backwards-incompatible-api-changes)
    
*   [Bug Fixes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-090-bug-fixes)
    
*   [Contributors](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#id5)
    

### Enhancements[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-090-enhancements "Permalink to this headline")

*   Added a timeout parameter to prevent infinite hangs ([GH790](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/790)
    )
    
*   Added AlphaVantage endpoint to get historical currency exchange rates ([GH764](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/764)
    )
    
*   Improved logging when rate limited ([GH745](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/745)
    )
    
*   Added daily historical data from Naver Finance ([GH722](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/722)
    )
    
*   Added the method `test` to the package to simplify running tests from an installation using
    

python -c "import pandas\_datareader; pandas\_datareader.test()"

### Backwards incompatible API changes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#backwards-incompatible-api-changes "Permalink to this headline")

*   Dropped support for Python 2.7. The minimum python version is now Python 3.6.
    
*   Removed Robinhood which no longer exists
    
*   Immediately deprecated AlphaVantage quote reader which used an end point that has been retired
    
*   Immediately deprecated Enigma which has substantially changed their business model and API
    
*   Immediately deprecated old symbol names for TSP to reflect the new website API
    

### Bug Fixes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-090-bug-fixes "Permalink to this headline")

*   Fix Yahoo Splits for change in format ([GH756](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/756)
    )
    
*   Fixed reading bond yields from Stooq ([GH752](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/752)
    )
    
*   Update TSP web scraper to new site ([GH740](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/740)
    )
    
*   Fixed EconDB reader to use session ([GH737](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/737)
    )
    
*   Fix reading futures data from Stooq ([GH718](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/718)
    )
    
*   Correct NASDAQ symbols fields link ([GH715](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/715)
    )
    
*   Fix Yahoo! actions bug due to change in split format ([GH755](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/755)
    )
    
*   Fix FutureWarning from pandas import ([GH762](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/762)
    )
    

### Contributors[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#id5 "Permalink to this headline")

*   Spencer Adams
    
*   Jesse Aldridge
    
*   Sumin Byeon
    
*   Patrick Collins
    
*   David Cottrell
    
*   Greg
    
*   Matthew Hall
    
*   Kirill Ikonnikov
    
*   Gábor Lipták
    
*   Kevin Sheppard
    
*   David Stephens
    
*   Eldon Allred
    

v0.8.0 (September 22, 2019)[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#v0-8-0-september-22-2019 "Permalink to this headline")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Highlights include:

*   A new connector for Econdb was introduced. Econdb provides aggregated economic data from 90+ official statistical agencies ([GH615](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/615)
    )
    
*   Migrated IEX readers to [IEX Cloud](https://iexcloud.io/)
    . All readers now require an API token (`IEX_API_KEY`) ([GH638](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/638)
    )
    
*   Removal of Google Finance and Morningstar, which were deprecated in 0.7.0
    
*   Immediate deprecation of Robinhood for quotes and historical data. Robinhood ended support for these endpoints in 1/2019
    

What’s new in v0.8.0

*   [Enhancements](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-080-enhancements)
    
*   [Backwards incompatible API changes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-080-api-breaking)
    
*   [Bug Fixes](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-080-bug-fixes)
    
*   [Contributors](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#id9)
    

### Enhancements[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-080-enhancements "Permalink to this headline")

*   Added Tiingo IEX Historical reader. ([GH619](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/619)
    )
    
*   Added support for Alpha Vantage intraday time series prices ([GH631](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/631)
    )
    
*   Up to 15 years of historical prices from IEX with new platform, IEX Cloud
    
*   Added testing on Python 3.7 ([GH667](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/667)
    )
    
*   Allow IEX to read less than 1 year of data ([GH649](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/649)
    )
    
*   Allow data download from Poland using stooq ([GH597](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/597)
    )
    
*   All time series readers now use a rolling default starting date (most are 5 years before the current date. Intraday readers are 3-5 days from the current date)
    

### Backwards incompatible API changes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-080-api-breaking "Permalink to this headline")

*   Immediate deprecation of Robinhood for quotes and historical data. Robinhood ended support for these endpoints in 1/2019. The Robinhood quotes and daily readers will raise an `ImmediateDeprecationError` when called.
    
*   Usage of all IEX readers requires an IEX Cloud API token, which can be passed as a parameter or stored in the environment variable `IEX_API_TOKEN`
    
*   Deprecated `access_key` in favor of `api_key` in `DataReader`. ([GH693](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/693)
    )
    

### Bug Fixes[¶](https://pandas-datareader.readthedocs.io/en/stable/whatsnew.html#whatsnew-080-bug-fixes "Permalink to this headline")

*   Fix Yahoo! actions issue where dividends are adjusted twice as a result of a change to the Yahoo! API. ([GH583](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/583)
    )
    
*   Fix AlphaVantage time series data ordering after provider switch to descending order (maintains ascending order for consistency). ([GH662](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/662)
    )
    
*   Refactored compatibility library to be independent of pandas version.
    
*   Fixed quarter value handling in JSDMX and OECD. ([GH685](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/685)
    )
    
*   Fixed a bug in `base` so that the reader does not error when response.encoding is `None`. ([GH674](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/674)
    )
    
*   Correct EcondbReader’s API URL format. ([GH670](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/670)
    )
    
*   Fix eurostat URL. ([GH669](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/669)
    )
    
*   Adjust Alphavantage time series reader to account for descending ordering. ([GH666](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/666)
    )
    
*   Fix bug in downloading index historical constituents. ([GH591](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/591)
    )
    
*   Fix a bug that occurs when an endpoint returns has no data for a date range. ([GH640](https://github.com/pydata/pandas-datareader/issues/640)
    )
